Disclaimer:
This project is a personal project will not and should not be used for commercial purposes

How to run:
1. Open with IntelliJ
2. Find ImagineAirApplication and run it
3. Should data be unavailable please run api /admin/create/bulk
4. /admin apis can only be used by authenticated users as admin
5. To login as admin use Postman
API: http://localhost:8080/api/v1/users/login
Request :
```json
{
  "email": "name20@gmail.com",
  "password": "password"
}
```

Response:
```json
{
    "errorMessage": null,
    "errorCode": null,
    "success": true,
    "value": {
        "id": null,
        "createdDate": null,
        "updatedDate": null,
        "firstName": "name 1",
        "lastName": "name 2",
        "email": "name20@gmail.com",
        "userRole": "ROLE_ADMIN",
        "gender": "male",
        "token": "eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJyb2xlcyI6WyJST0xFX0FETUlOIl0sImlzcyI6Im5hbWUyMEBnbWFpbC5jb20iLCJleHAiOjE3MzE1MDMzNjUsImlhdCI6MTczMTQ5OTc2NX0.MlTQXdhsH8oCNgm-59cHJCxbkCfTuOBRDuZ0y3jgNAM",
        "phoneNo": "08129121111",
        "imageUrl": null
    }
}
```


6. Api for create data bulk:
http://localhost:8080/api/v1/flights/admin/create/bulk
Params: days: int
Response:
